                    </h2>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary">
                   <a class="omnitrack" data-omnilink="hero-sum" data-omnilocation="hero" href="/labor/healthcare-workers-covid-19-vaccine-demand-still-outpaces-supply">
                    Travel nurses, home care workers and others who aren't affiliated with hospitals or long-term care facilities have been caught in scramble for COVID-19 vaccination. Only 52% of front-line healthcareworkers have received at least one dose.

                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/hospital-systems/sanford-invests-300-million-rural-health">

                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">

                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/awards/health-care-hall-fame-2021">
                    Health Care Hall of Fame - 2021
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   <p>
                    The Health Care Hall of Fame award is one of healthcare industrys most prestigious honors. A partnership between Modern Healthcare and the American College of Healthcare Executives (ACHE), the program was created to recognize the men and women who have made extraordinary strides, outstanding and lasting contributions to the healthcare industry.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Each year, healthcare luminaries are inducted into the Modern Healthcare Hall of Fame. Since 1988, one hundred twelve (112) healthcare visionaries, original thinkers and leaders have been honored with this coveted distinction. A plaque to commemorate the honor is installed in the Health Care Hall of Fame, prominently displayed at Pennsylvania Hospital, the nations first hospital founded by Benjamin Franklin and Thomas Bond.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    For program eligibility, key dates and requirements,
                    <a href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/nominate/health-care-hall-of-fame">
                     click here
                    </a>
                    for more details.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/awards/health-care-hall-of-fame-past-inductees">
                     View the Past Hall of Fame Inductees
                    </a>
                    .
                   </p>
                  </div>
                  <div class="feature-article-category-details">
                   <a class="cta pull-right" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/awards/health-care-hall-fame-2021">
                    View the Honoree
                   </a>
                  </div>

                  <div class="feature-article-category-timestamp">
                   <span class="feature-article-category">
                    <a href="/mergers-acquisitions">
                     Mergers &amp; Acquisitions
                    </a>
                   </span>
                   <span class="text-gray divider-gray article-update-time" data-lastupdated="update--1616169956">
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/mergers-acquisitions/hospitals-ask-doj-probe-unitedhealths-change-healthcare-acquisition">
                    Hospitals ask DOJ to probe UnitedHealth's Change Healthcare acquisition
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   The American Hospital Association warned regulators that the move could reduce competition in health IT services and give UnitedHealth Group too much control over health data.
                  </div>

                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/insurance/two-thirds-insurers-32-states-now-have-copay-accumulators-study-says">
                    Two-thirds of insurers in 32 states now have copay accumulators, study says
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   Most health plans across the country include an opaque policy that prevents drug manufacturer coupons and copay assistance from counting against a plan's deductible or out-of-pocket limit, which could affect access to treatment.

                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.modernhealthcare.com/policy/critics-doctors-note-vaccine-unfairly-penalizing-poor">
                    Critics: Doctor's note for vaccine unfairly penalizing poor
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   <p>
                    Florida requires little more than a doctor's signature for individuals with certain conditions to receive a COVID-19 vaccine. But critics say it's an onerous added barrier for minorities and low-income residents without health insurance or access to a doctor.
                   </p>
